Here is the situation:\\ \tt \\ \tt WHAT: Things at places\\ \tt LEFT: daisy\\ \tt RIGHT: strawberry\\ \tt TOP: pens\\ \tt BOTTOM: mirror\\ \tt CENTER: aluminium\\ \tt NORTHWEST: eyeliner\\ \tt NORTHEAST: banjo\\ \tt SOUTHWEST: mug\\ \tt SOUTHEAST: mimosa\\ \tt HERE: watermelon\\ \tt THERE: camellia\\ \tt NOWHERE: cutlery\\ \tt EVERYWHERE: eagle\\ \tt INSIDE: mango\\ \tt OUTSIDE: tambourine\\ \tt \\ \tt Questions from the questioner will start with QUESTIONER. Please reply in the form: ANSWER: <one sentence>\\ \tt \\ \tt I will also ask you questions. These questions will start with ME: . Please answer these questions with: ASIDE: <one sentence>\\ \tt \\ \tt Important: Give short, direct answers!\\ \tt \\ \tt Let us start. 
	  }

	   }
